  @Override
  public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
    if (e.getSource() == mainPageButton[0]) {
      mainFrame.remove(mainPage);
      mainFrame.add(page_A[1]);
      mainFrame.add(pageMenuBar_A, BorderLayout.NORTH);
      mainFrame.revalidate();
      mainFrame.repaint();
      pageNo_A.setSelectedIndex(1);
    }
    if (e.getSource() == mainPageButton[1]) {
      mainFrame.remove(mainPage);
      mainFrame.add(page_B[1]);
      mainFrame.add(pageMenuBar_B, BorderLayout.NORTH);
      mainFrame.revalidate();
      mainFrame.repaint();
      pageNo_B.setSelectedIndex(1);
    }
    if (e.getSource() == mainPageButton[2]) {
      mainFrame.remove(mainPage);
      mainFrame.add(settings);
      mainFrame.add(settingsMenuBar, BorderLayout.NORTH);
      mainFrame.revalidate();
      mainFrame.repaint();
    }
    if (e.getSource() == mainPageButton[3]) {
      System.exit(0);
    }
    if (e.getSource() == homePageButton_A && mainPage.getParent() == null) {
      mainFrame.remove(pageMenuBar_A);
      for (int i = 1; i < 150; i++) {
        mainFrame.remove(page_A[i]);
      }
      mainFrame.add(mainPage);
      mainFrame.revalidate();
      mainFrame.repaint();
    }
    if (e.getSource() == homePageButton_B && mainPage.getParent() == null) {
      mainFrame.remove(pageMenuBar_B);
      for (int i = 1; i < 100; i++) {
        mainFrame.remove(page_B[i]);
      }
      mainFrame.add(mainPage);
      mainFrame.revalidate();
      mainFrame.repaint();
    }
    if (e.getSource() == settingsHomePageButton && mainPage.getParent() == null) {
      mainFrame.remove(settingsMenuBar);
      mainFrame.remove(settings);
      mainFrame.add(mainPage);
      mainFrame.revalidate();
      mainFrame.repaint();
    }
    if (styleRadioButton[0].isSelected() && (!styleRadioButton[1].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[2].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[3].isSelected()) && !styleRadioButton[4].isSelected()) {
      try {
        UIManager.setLookAndFeel("javax.swing.plaf.metal.MetalLookAndFeel");
      } catch (ClassNotFoundException | InstantiationException | IllegalAccessException |
        UnsupportedLookAndFeelException e1) {
        e1.printStackTrace();
      }
      swingUtilitiesUpdateComponentTreeUI();
    }
    if (styleRadioButton[1].isSelected() && (!styleRadioButton[0].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[2].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[3].isSelected()) && !styleRadioButton[4].isSelected()) {
      try {
        UIManager.setLookAndFeel("com.sun.java.swing.plaf.motif.MotifLookAndFeel");
      } catch (ClassNotFoundException | InstantiationException | IllegalAccessException |
        UnsupportedLookAndFeelException e1) {
        e1.printStackTrace();
      }
      swingUtilitiesUpdateComponentTreeUI();
    }
    if (styleRadioButton[2].isSelected() && (!styleRadioButton[0].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[1].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[3].isSelected()) && !styleRadioButton[4].isSelected()) {
      try {
        UIManager.setLookAndFeel("javax.swing.plaf.nimbus.NimbusLookAndFeel");
      } catch (ClassNotFoundException | InstantiationException | IllegalAccessException |
        UnsupportedLookAndFeelException e1) {
        e1.printStackTrace();
      }
      swingUtilitiesUpdateComponentTreeUI();
    }
    if (styleRadioButton[3].isSelected() && (!styleRadioButton[0].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[1].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[2].isSelected()) && !styleRadioButton[4].isSelected()) {
      try {
        UIManager.setLookAndFeel("com.sun.java.swing.plaf.windows.WindowsLookAndFeel");
      } catch (ClassNotFoundException | InstantiationException | IllegalAccessException |
        UnsupportedLookAndFeelException e1) {
        e1.printStackTrace();
      }
      swingUtilitiesUpdateComponentTreeUI();
    }
    if (styleRadioButton[4].isSelected() && (!styleRadioButton[0].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[1].isSelected() && !styleRadioButton[2].isSelected()) && !styleRadioButton[3].isSelected()) {
      try {
        UIManager.setLookAndFeel("com.sun.java.swing.plaf.windows.WindowsClassicLookAndFeel");
      } catch (ClassNotFoundException | InstantiationException | IllegalAccessException |
        UnsupportedLookAndFeelException e1) {
        e1.printStackTrace();
      }
      swingUtilitiesUpdateComponentTreeUI();
    }
  }
  @Override
  public void mouseEntered(MouseEvent e) {
    if (e.getSource() == flag[0]) {
      EU_clip.setMicrosecondPosition(0);
      EU_clip.start();
    }
    if (e.getSource() == flag[1]) {
      tarantellaNapoletanaClip.setMicrosecondPosition(0);
      tarantellaNapoletanaClip.start();
    }
    if (e.getSource() == flag[2]) {
      czerwoneJagodyClip.setMicrosecondPosition(0);
      czerwoneJagodyClip.start();
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
      if (e.getSource() == flag[i]) {
        mainFrame.setCursor(Cursor.getPredefinedCursor(Cursor.CROSSHAIR_CURSOR));
      }
    }
    for (int i = 1; i <= 1488; i++) {
      if (e.getSource() == PL_wyraz_A[i]) {
        PL_wyraz_A[i].setBackground(gold);
        PL_wyraz_A[i].setBorder(BorderFactory.createLoweredSoftBevelBorder());
        PL_clip_A[i].setMicrosecondPosition(0);
        PL_clip_A[i].start();
      }
      if (e.getSource() == IT_espr_A[i]) {
        IT_espr_A[i].setBackground(gold);
        IT_espr_A[i].setBorder(BorderFactory.createLoweredSoftBevelBorder());
        IT_clip_A[i].setMicrosecondPosition(0);
        IT_clip_A[i].start();
      }
    }
    for (int i = 1; i <= 464; i++) {
      if (e.getSource() == PL_wyraz_B[i]) {
        PL_wyraz_B[i].setBackground(gold);
        PL_wyraz_B[i].setBorder(BorderFactory.createLoweredBevelBorder());
        PL_clip_B[i].setMicrosecondPosition(0);
        PL_clip_B[i].start();
      }
      if (e.getSource() == IT_espr_B[i]) {
        IT_espr_B[i].setBackground(gold);
        IT_espr_B[i].setBorder(BorderFactory.createLoweredBevelBorder());
        IT_clip_B[i].start();
        IT_clip_B[i].setMicrosecondPosition(0);
      }
    }
  }
  public void mouseExited(MouseEvent e) {
    if (e.getSource() == flag[0]) {
      EU_clip.stop();
    }
    if (e.getSource() == flag[1]) {
      tarantellaNapoletanaClip.stop();
    }
    if (e.getSource() == flag[2]) {
      czerwoneJagodyClip.stop();
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
      if (e.getSource() == flag[i]) {
        mainFrame.setCursor(Cursor.getPredefinedCursor(Cursor.DEFAULT_CURSOR));
      }
    }
    for (int i = 1; i <= 1488; i++) {
      if (e.getSource() == PL_wyraz_A[i]) {
        PL_wyraz_A[i].setBackground(null);
        PL_wyraz_A[i].setBorder(BorderFactory.createRaisedSoftBevelBorder());
        PL_clip_A[i].stop();
      }
      if (e.getSource() == IT_espr_A[i]) {
        IT_espr_A[i].setBackground(null);
        IT_espr_A[i].setBorder(BorderFactory.createRaisedSoftBevelBorder());
        IT_clip_A[i].stop();
      }
    }
    for (int i = 1; i <= 464; i++) {
      if (e.getSource() == PL_wyraz_B[i]) {
        PL_wyraz_B[i].setBackground(null);
        PL_wyraz_B[i].setBorder(BorderFactory.createRaisedBevelBorder());
        PL_clip_B[i].stop();
      }
      if (e.getSource() == IT_espr_B[i]) {
        IT_espr_B[i].setBackground(null);
        IT_espr_B[i].setBorder(BorderFactory.createRaisedBevelBorder());
        IT_clip_B[i].stop();
      }
    }
  }

  public void pageNo() {
    pageNo_A = new JComboBox < String > ();
    comboBoxFont = new Font("Microsoft Sans Serif", Font.PLAIN, 25);
    pageNo_A.addItemListener(new ItemListener() {
      public void itemStateChanged(ItemEvent e) {
        if (pageNo_A.getSelectedIndex() == 1) {
          for (int i = 2; i < 150; i++) {
            mainFrame.remove(page_A[i]);
          }
          mainFrame.add(page_A[1]);
          mainFrame.revalidate();
          mainFrame.repaint();
        }
        if (pageNo_A.getSelectedIndex() == 2) {
          for (int i = 1; i < 150; i++) {
            if (i == 2) {
              continue;
            }
            mainFrame.remove(page_A[i]);
          }
          mainFrame.add(page_A[2]);
          mainFrame.revalidate();
          mainFrame.repaint();
        }
        if (pageNo_A.getSelectedIndex() == 3) {
          for (int i = 1; i < 150; i++) {
            if (i == 3) {
              continue;
            }
            mainFrame.remove(page_A[i]);
          }
          mainFrame.add(page_A[3]);
          mainFrame.revalidate();
          mainFrame.repaint();
        }
        if (pageNo_A.getSelectedIndex() == 4) {
          for (int i = 1; i < 150; i++) {
            if (i == 4) {
              continue;
            }
            mainFrame.remove(page_A[i]);
          }
          mainFrame.add(page_A[4]);
          mainFrame.revalidate();
          mainFrame.repaint();

  public void swingUtilitiesUpdateComponentTreeUI() {
    SwingUtilities.updateComponentTreeUI(mainFrame);
    for (int i = 1; i < 150; i++) {
      SwingUtilities.updateComponentTreeUI(page_A[i]);
    }
    for (int i = 1; i < 100; i++) {
      SwingUtilities.updateComponentTreeUI(page_B[i]);
    }
  }
